Part 17 — Noun System Deep Study

(संज्ञा प्रणाली का गहन अध्ययन)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने noun का basic समझा था।

अब हम noun को detail में समझेंगे।

क्योंकि sentence में:

व्यक्ति

स्थान

वस्तु

विचार

गुण

अवस्था

सबको व्यक्त करने के लिए noun का उपयोग होता है।

---

What is a Noun?

English Definition

A noun is the name of any person, place, thing, idea, or quality.

---

Hindi Definition

जो शब्द किसी व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का नाम बताए, उसे noun कहते हैं।

---

Important Understanding

Traditional English grammar के अनुसार noun के पाँच भेद माने जाते हैं।

लेकिन modern English grammar के अनुसार noun के मुख्यतः तीन functional classification माने जाते हैं।

---

Traditional Classification of Noun

1. Proper Noun

2. Common Noun

3. Collective Noun

4. Material Noun

5. Abstract Noun

---

Modern Classification of Noun

1. Proper Noun

2. Countable Noun

3. Uncountable Noun

---

Important Understanding

Modern grammar में:

Proper noun अलग category बना रहा।

Common noun और collective noun को countable noun में रखा गया।

Material noun और abstract noun को uncountable noun में रखा गया।

---

1. Proper Noun

(व्यक्तिवाचक संज्ञा)

English Definition

The name of a particular or specific person, place, or thing is called a proper noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा किसी विशेष व्यक्ति, स्थान या वस्तु का नाम बताए, उसे Proper Noun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

Ram → राम

Mohan → मोहन

Nepal → नेपाल

India → भारत

Koshi Patti → कोशी पट्टी

---

Important Understanding

Proper noun:

specific होता है

और सामान्यतः capital letter से शुरू होता है।

---

2. Common Noun

(जातिवाचक संज्ञा)

English Definition

A name given in common to every person, place, or thing of the same kind or class is called a common noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा एक ही प्रकार या वर्ग के सभी व्यक्ति, स्थान या वस्तुओं के लिए सामान्य रूप से प्रयोग की जाए, उसे Common Noun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

man → आदमी

country → देश

phone → फोन

teacher → शिक्षक

---

Important Understanding

Common noun: किसी specific नाम की बात नहीं करता, बल्कि पूरे वर्ग की बात करता है।

---

3. Collective Noun

(समूहवाचक संज्ञा)

English Definition

The noun made of a collection of the same type of things is called a collective noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा समान प्रकार की वस्तुओं, व्यक्तियों या जीवों के समूह का बोध कराए, उसे Collective Noun कहते हैं।

---

Important Note

Collective noun का निर्माण सामान्यतः common noun से होता है।

---

Examples

a class → students का समूह

a team → players का समूह

a herd → animals का झुंड

a family → family members का समूह

a crew → sailors का समूह

---

Important Understanding

Collective noun: एक शब्द होता है, लेकिन उसके अंदर कई सदस्य शामिल होते हैं।

---

4. Material Noun

(पदार्थवाचक संज्ञा)

English Definition

The name of a material or substance that is used as raw material for other things is called a material noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा किसी पदार्थ या सामग्री का नाम बताए जिससे दूसरी वस्तुएँ बनती हैं, उसे Material Noun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

wheat → गेहूँ

sugar → चीनी

flour → आटा

milk → दूध

gold → सोना

---

Example Sentence

This ring is made of gold.

---

5. Abstract Noun

(भाववाचक संज्ञा)

English Definition

A noun that refers to an idea, feeling, quality, or state and not to a physical object is called an abstract noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा किसी विचार, गुण, भावना या अवस्था का बोध कराए, न कि किसी भौतिक वस्तु का, उसे Abstract Noun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

kindness → दयालुता

honesty → ईमानदारी

wisdom → बुद्धिमानी

freedom → स्वतंत्रता

---

Important Understanding

Abstract nouns:

महसूस किए जा सकते हैं

लेकिन छुए नहीं जा सकते।

---

Modern Classification According to Function

अब modern grammar के अनुसार noun को function के आधार पर भी समझा जाता है।

---

1. Proper Noun

विशेष व्यक्ति, स्थान या वस्तु का नाम।

Examples:

Ram

Mohan

Samsung

Nokia

---

2. Countable Noun

(गणनीय संज्ञा)

English Definition

The noun that can be counted is called a countable noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जिस संज्ञा को गिना जा सके, उसे Countable Noun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

apple → apples

book → books

pen → pens

mango → mangoes

---

3. Uncountable Noun

(अगणनीय संज्ञा)

English Definition

The noun that cannot normally be counted individually is called an uncountable noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जिस संज्ञा को सामान्यतः अलग-अलग गिना न जा सके, उसे Uncountable Noun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

oil → तेल

rice → चावल

sugar → चीनी

water → पानी

---

Number System

(वचन प्रणाली)

English Definition

The counting of things is called number.

---

Hindi Definition

वस्तुओं की गिनती को वचन कहते हैं।

---

Types of Number

1. Singular Number

2. Plural Number

---

Singular Number

(एकवचन)

English Definition

The noun that refers to one person, place, thing, idea, or quality is called singular number.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा एक व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का बोध कराए, उसे Singular Number कहते हैं।

---

Examples

boy

girl

book

apple

---

Plural Number

(बहुवचन)

English Definition

The noun that refers to more than one person, place, thing, idea, or quality is called plural number.

---

Hindi Definition

जो संज्ञा एक से अधिक व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का बोध कराए, उसे Plural Number कहते हैं।

---

Examples

boys

girls

books

apples

---

Important Understanding

Uncountable nouns सामान्यतः singular माने जाते हैं।

---

Examples

water

milk

oil

air

---

Exception

five packets of milk

five bags of rice

यहाँ: count material नहीं, container count हो रहा है।

---

Proper Noun and Number

Proper noun सामान्यतः singular होते हैं।

---

Examples

Ram

Krishna

The Sun

The Moon

---

But Sometimes Proper Nouns Become Plural

The Smiths

→ Smith परिवार

The Himalayas

→ हिमालय की पर्वत श्रृंखलाएँ

---

Important Rule

All words ending with “s” are not plural.

---

Examples

mathematics

physics

economics

news

headquarters

series

---

Some Nouns Are Always Plural

clothes

trousers

scissors

glasses

binoculars

---

Rules of Singular and Plural

Rule 1

यदि noun के अंत में:

s

sh

ch

x

z

हो, तो “es” जोड़कर plural बनाते हैं।

---

Examples

class → classes

bench → benches

bus → buses

dress → dresses

quiz → quizzes

---

Rule 2

यदि noun के अंत में “o” हो और उससे पहले consonant हो, तो “es” जोड़ते हैं।

---

Examples

hero → heroes

potato → potatoes

tomato → tomatoes

---

Rule 3

यदि “o” से पहले vowel हो, तो सामान्यतः “s” जोड़ते हैं।

---

Examples

radio → radios

video → videos

studio → studios

---

Rule 4

यदि noun के अंत में “y” हो और उससे पहले consonant हो, तो “y” हटाकर “ies” जोड़ते हैं।

---

Examples

city → cities

baby → babies

party → parties

family → families

---

Rule 5

यदि “y” से पहले vowel हो, तो केवल “s” जोड़ते हैं।

---

Examples

boy → boys

toy → toys

day → days

---

Irregular Plurals

man → men

woman → women

tooth → teeth

foot → feet

mouse → mice

goose → geese

---

Number System Awareness

Cardinal Number

Quantity बताता है।

Examples:

1, 2, 3, 4

---

Ordinal Number

Position बताता है।

Examples:

first

second

third

fourth

---

Noun Phrase Awareness

English Definition

The group of words that acts like a noun in a sentence is called a noun phrase.

---

Hindi Definition

शब्दों का ऐसा समूह जो वाक्य में noun की तरह कार्य करे, noun phrase कहलाता है।

---

Examples

the boy

the tall boy

the tall boy in blue shirt

---

Noun Phrase vs Clause

Noun Phrase

main verb नहीं होती

noun structure होता है

Example: the tall boy

---

Clause

अपना subject और verb दोनों होते हैं

Example: because it is hot

---

Final Easy Rule

अगर:

केवल नाम और विशेषता हो → noun phrase

अगर:

subject + verb दोनों हों → clause।

Part 18 — Pronoun System

(सर्वनाम प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, Part 17 में हमने noun को detail में समझा।

अब एक समस्या आती है।

अगर noun को बार-बार repeat करें, तो sentence भारी और awkward लगने लगता है।

Example:

Ram is a good boy. Ram goes to school daily. Ram studies hard.

यह sentence बार-बार “Ram” repeat कर रहा है।

इस repetition को रोकने के लिए: Pronoun का उपयोग किया जाता है।

---

What is a Pronoun?

English Definition

The word that is used instead of a noun or noun phrase to avoid its repetition is called a pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो संज्ञा या संज्ञा वाक्यांश की जगह उसकी पुनरावृत्ति को रोकने के लिए उपयोग किया जाता है, pronoun कहलाता है।

---

Examples

I → मैं

We → हम

You → तुम / आप

He → वह

She → वह

It → यह / वह

They → वे

---

Example Sentence

Ram is a good boy. He studies daily.

यहाँ: “He” Ram की जगह आया है।

इसलिए: He = pronoun

---

Noun Phrase and Pronoun Connection

Pronoun केवल noun की जगह ही नहीं, noun phrase की जगह भी आ सकता है।

---

Example

The tall boy with blue shirt is my friend. He is very smart.

यहाँ: “He” पूरे noun phrase की जगह आया है।

---

Important Understanding

Pronoun का मुख्य कार्य:

repetition रोकना

sentence को छोटा बनाना

communication को smooth बनाना

है।

---

Types of Pronoun

अब हम pronoun के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

---

1. Personal Pronoun

(पुरुषवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun used for persons or things is called a personal pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम व्यक्ति या वस्तु के लिए प्रयोग किया जाए, उसे Personal Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

I

We

You

He

She

It

They

---

Example Sentences

I am a teacher.

→ मैं शिक्षक हूँ।

She is happy.

→ वह खुश है।

They are playing.

→ वे खेल रहे हैं।

---

Person System

First Person

Speaker

I, We

---

Second Person

Listener

You

---

Third Person

Others

He, She, It, They

---

2. Reflexive Pronoun

(निजवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun that reflects the action back to the subject is called a reflexive pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम क्रिया का प्रभाव वापस subject पर दिखाए, उसे Reflexive Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

myself

yourself

himself

herself

themselves

---

Example Sentences

I hurt myself.

→ मैंने स्वयं को चोट पहुँचाई।

She looked at herself in the mirror.

→ उसने स्वयं को दर्पण में देखा।

---

Important Understanding

Reflexive pronoun: subject और object को same व्यक्ति बनाता है।

---

3. Emphatic Pronoun

(बलवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun used to emphasize a noun or pronoun is called an emphatic pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम किसी noun या pronoun पर बल देने के लिए प्रयोग किया जाए, उसे Emphatic Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

I myself did the work.

→ मैंने स्वयं काम किया।

The principal himself came here.

→ प्रधानाचार्य स्वयं यहाँ आए।

---

Important Understanding

Reflexive और emphatic pronoun के forms same होते हैं, लेकिन function अलग होता है।

---

4. Demonstrative Pronoun

(संकेतवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun used to point out a person or thing is called a demonstrative pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम किसी व्यक्ति या वस्तु की ओर संकेत करे, उसे Demonstrative Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

this

that

these

those

---

Example Sentences

This is my book.

→ यह मेरी किताब है।

Those are students.

→ वे छात्र हैं।

---

Important Understanding

Near

this, these

---

Far

that, those

---

5. Relative Pronoun

(संबंधवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun that relates a clause to a noun or pronoun is called a relative pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम किसी clause को noun या pronoun से जोड़े, उसे Relative Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

who

whom

whose

which

that

---

Example Sentence

The boy who is standing there is my friend.

यहाँ: “who” boy और clause को जोड़ रहा है।

---

6. Distributive Pronoun

(वितरणवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun that refers to persons or things one at a time is called a distributive pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम व्यक्तियों या वस्तुओं को एक-एक करके दर्शाए, उसे Distributive Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

each

either

neither

---

Example Sentences

Each of the boys was present.

Neither of the answers is correct.

---

7. Reciprocal Pronoun

(परस्परवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun used to show mutual action or relationship is called a reciprocal pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम परस्पर संबंध या क्रिया को व्यक्त करे, उसे Reciprocal Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

each other

one another

---

Example Sentences

The two friends helped each other.

The students greeted one another.

---

8. Interrogative Pronoun

(प्रश्नवाचक सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun used for asking questions is called an interrogative pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम प्रश्न पूछने के लिए प्रयोग किया जाए, उसे Interrogative Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

who

whom

whose

what

which

---

Example Sentences

Who are you?

→ तुम कौन हो?

Which is your book?

→ तुम्हारी किताब कौन-सी है?

---

9. Indefinite Pronoun

(अनिश्चित सर्वनाम)

English Definition

The pronoun that refers to persons or things in a general or indefinite way is called an indefinite pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो सर्वनाम किसी व्यक्ति या वस्तु का अनिश्चित रूप से बोध कराए, उसे Indefinite Pronoun कहते हैं।

---

Examples

someone

anyone

everyone

nothing

something

---

Example Sentences

Someone is knocking at the door.

Everybody likes honesty.

---

Pronoun Agreement

Pronoun का:

number

person

gender

अपने noun के अनुसार होना चाहिए।

---

Example

Ram lost his book. ✅

Ram lost her book. ❌

---

Important Understanding

Pronoun हमेशा: जिस noun की जगह आता है, उससे logically match करना चाहिए।

---

Common Mistakes

कुछ students:

pronoun और noun का agreement बिगाड़ देते हैं।

singular noun के साथ plural pronoun लगा देते हैं।

---

Tiny Practice

बताइए नीचे दिए गए pronouns किस प्रकार के हैं:

1. He

2. Myself

3. This

4. Who

5. Each other

Part 19 — Adjective System

(विशेषण प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, Part 18 में हमने pronoun पढ़ा।

अब हम adjective समझेंगे।

Noun या pronoun केवल नाम बताते हैं।

लेकिन:

वह कैसा है?

कितना है?

कौन-सा है?

किस प्रकार का है?

यह जानकारी adjective देता है।

---

What is an Adjective?

English Definition

The word that describes or modifies a noun, pronoun, or noun phrase is called an adjective.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो संज्ञा, सर्वनाम या संज्ञा वाक्यांश की विशेषता बताए या उसके अर्थ को और स्पष्ट करे, adjective कहलाता है।

---

Examples

red car

→ लाल गाड़ी

good boy

→ अच्छा लड़का

smart girl

→ होशियार लड़की

---

Important Understanding

Adjective: noun/pronoun के बारे में extra information देता है।

---

Example Understanding

red car

“red” car की विशेषता बता रहा है।

---

good boy

“good” boy के बारे में बता रहा है कि लड़का कैसा है।

---

smart girl

“smart” girl की quality बता रहा है।

---

Adjective and Noun Phrase

Adjective, noun phrase का भी part बन सकता है।

---

Example

the tall boy

→ लंबा लड़का

the beautiful red car

→ सुंदर लाल गाड़ी

---

Important Understanding

जब adjective noun के साथ जुड़ता है, तो पूरा समूह noun phrase बन सकता है।

---

Kinds of Adjective

अब हम adjective के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

---

1. Adjective of Quality

(गुणवाचक विशेषण)

English Definition

The adjective that tells the quality or nature of a noun or pronoun is called an adjective of quality.

---

Hindi Definition

जो विशेषण किसी noun या pronoun के गुण या स्वभाव का बोध कराए, उसे Adjective of Quality कहते हैं।

---

Examples

good boy

beautiful girl

honest man

brave soldier

---

Explanation

good → लड़का कैसा है

beautiful → लड़की कैसी है

---

2. Adjective of Quantity

(परिमाणवाचक विशेषण)

English Definition

The adjective that tells the quantity of something is called an adjective of quantity.

---

Hindi Definition

जो विशेषण किसी वस्तु की मात्रा का बोध कराए, उसे Adjective of Quantity कहते हैं।

---

Examples

some water

much milk

little sugar

enough food

---

Important Understanding

यह exact number नहीं बताता, सिर्फ मात्रा का अंदाज़ा बताता है।

---

3. Adjective of Number

(संख्यावाचक विशेषण)

English Definition

The adjective that tells the number or order of nouns is called an adjective of number.

---

Hindi Definition

जो विशेषण संज्ञा की संख्या या क्रम का बोध कराए, उसे Adjective of Number कहते हैं।

---

Examples

one boy

two girls

first chapter

second player

---

Important Understanding

Cardinal Number

Quantity बताता है।

Examples: one, two, three

---

Ordinal Number

Position बताता है।

Examples: first, second, third

---

Difference Between Quantity and Number

Quantity

अंदाज़ा

some water

---

Number

Exact counting

three books

---

4. Demonstrative Adjective

(संकेतवाचक विशेषण)

English Definition

The adjective that points out a noun is called a demonstrative adjective.

---

Hindi Definition

जो विशेषण किसी noun की ओर संकेत करे, उसे Demonstrative Adjective कहते हैं।

---

Examples

this book

that boy

these apples

those houses

---

Important Understanding

Near

this, these

---

Far

that, those

---

Demonstrative Adjective vs Demonstrative Pronoun

Demonstrative Adjective

this book

यहाँ: book noun मौजूद है।

---

Demonstrative Pronoun

This is my book.

यहाँ: noun नहीं है।

---

5. Possessive Adjective

(अधिकारवाचक विशेषण)

English Definition

The adjective that shows possession or ownership is called a possessive adjective.

---

Hindi Definition

जो विशेषण अधिकार या संबंध का बोध कराए, उसे Possessive Adjective कहते हैं।

---

Examples

my book

your pen

his car

their house

---

6. Interrogative Adjective

(प्रश्नवाचक विशेषण)

English Definition

The adjective used with a noun to ask questions is called an interrogative adjective.

---

Hindi Definition

जो विशेषण noun के साथ प्रश्न पूछने के लिए प्रयोग किया जाए, उसे Interrogative Adjective कहते हैं।

---

Examples

which book

what subject

whose bag

---

Example Sentences

Which book is yours?

What language do you speak?

---

Degree of Adjective

(विशेषण की डिग्री)

Adjective की तुलना तीन स्तरों पर की जाती है।

---

1. Positive Degree

सामान्य अवस्था।

Example:

Ram is tall.

---

2. Comparative Degree

दो लोगों/वस्तुओं की तुलना।

Example:

Ram is taller than Mohan.

---

3. Superlative Degree

सबसे अधिक तुलना।

Example:

Ram is the tallest boy in the class.

---

More Examples

smart

smarter

smartest

good

better

best

---

Important Understanding

सभी adjectives degree नहीं बनाते।

---

Adjective Order

(विशेषणों का क्रम)

English में कई adjectives एक साथ आने पर उनका एक सामान्य क्रम होता है।

---

Example

a beautiful small red car

---

सामान्य क्रम

Opinion → Size → Color → Noun

---

Example Breakdown

beautiful → opinion

small → size

red → color

car → noun

---

Adjective vs Adverb

Adjective

noun/pronoun को modify करता है।

Example:

He is a smart boy.

---

Adverb

verb/adjective/adverb को modify करता है।

Example:

He runs quickly.

---

Important Understanding

Adjective: “कैसा?”

Adverb: “कैसे?”

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern grammar में:

determiner

article

quantifier

numeral

को कई scholars adjective family का हिस्सा मानते हैं।

आगे grammar में इसे detail में पढ़ेंगे।

---

Common Mistakes

कुछ students:

adjective और adverb को confuse कर देते हैं।

noun की जगह verb को modify कर देते हैं।

---

Tiny Practice

बताइए नीचे दिए गए adjectives किस प्रकार के हैं:

1. beautiful

2. some

3. three

4. this

5. my

Part 20 — Modern Adjective Family Expansion

(आधुनिक विशेषण परिवार विस्तार)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, Part 19 में हमने adjective system पढ़ा।

अब हम grammar के एक बहुत important modern concept को समझेंगे।

पुराने समय में:

article

determiner

quantifier

numeral

को adjective family के अंदर ही पढ़ाया जाता था।

लेकिन modern grammar में: इनकी अलग विशेषताओं और अलग rules की वजह से इन्हें अलग पहचान दी गई।

---

Important Historical Understanding

पुराने समय में adjective एक बहुत बड़ा परिवार था।

उसके अंदर:

determiner

article

quantifier

numeral

सब शामिल थे।

लेकिन आधुनिक grammar scholars ने देखा कि: इनका function और grammar rules अलग हैं।

इसलिए: इन्हें अलग categories की तरह पढ़ाना अधिक सही माना गया।

---

Modern Adjective Family

1. Determiner

2. Article

3. Quantifier

4. Numeral

---

1. Determiner

(निर्धारक)

English Definition

A word that comes before a noun to identify it or point it out is called a determiner.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो noun से पहले आकर उसे पहचानने या उसकी ओर संकेत करने का कार्य करे, determiner कहलाता है।

---

Examples

this boy

that house

these books

those students

---

Important Understanding

Determiner: noun की सीमा तय करता है।

यह बताता है:

कौन-सा noun

किस noun की बात हो रही है

---

Important Rule

Determiner सामान्यतः noun से पहले आता है।

---

Examples

this book

my pen

those boys

---

Determiner vs Adjective

Adjective

quality बताता है।

Examples:

red car

smart boy

---

Determiner

noun की पहचान/सीमा बताता है।

Examples:

this book

that girl

---

Important Understanding

Adjective

कैसा?

---

Determiner

कौन-सा?

---

Why Modern Grammar Separated Determiners

क्योंकि: determiners के rules adjectives से अलग हैं।

---

Rule 1 — Degree Rule

Adjective: degree बदल सकता है।

Examples:

smart

smarter

smartest

---

लेकिन determiner: degree नहीं बदलता।

❌ thiser

❌ thisest

---

Rule 2 — Position Rule

Determiner सामान्यतः सबसे पहले आता है।

Example:

this beautiful girl

---

यहाँ: this → determiner

beautiful → adjective

---

Rule 3 — Repetition Rule

एक noun के साथ: कई adjectives आ सकते हैं।

Example:

a tall handsome smart boy

---

लेकिन: दो determiners सामान्यतः साथ नहीं आते।

❌ the this boy

❌ a my book

---

2. Article

(आर्टिकल)

English Definition

An article is a word that comes before a noun to indicate whether the noun is general or specific.

---

Hindi Definition

Article वह शब्द है जो noun से पहले आकर यह बताता है कि noun सामान्य है या विशेष।

---

Types of Articles

1. Indefinite Articles

a

an

---

2. Definite Article

the

---

Use of “A”

“A” का प्रयोग singular countable noun से पहले होता है जो consonant sound से शुरू हो।

---

Examples

a boy

a cat

a university

---

Important Understanding

university: vowel letter से शुरू है, लेकिन sound: “यु”

आ रही है।

इसलिए: a university

---

Use of “An”

“An” का प्रयोग singular countable noun से पहले होता है जो vowel sound से शुरू हो।

---

Examples

an apple

an egg

an honest man

---

Important Understanding

honest: “H” silent है।

इसलिए: an honest man

---

Definite Article “The”

“The” specific noun को दिखाता है।

---

Examples

the sun

the moon

the Taj Mahal

---

General vs Specific

a girl

→ कोई भी लड़की

the girl

→ कोई विशेष लड़की

---

Pronunciation of “The”

“The” = द

जब अगला word consonant sound से शुरू हो।

Example:

the boy

the Hindu

---

“The” = दी

जब अगला word vowel sound से शुरू हो।

Example:

the elephant

the apple

---

Article vs Adjective

Similarity

दोनों noun के बारे में information देते हैं।

---

Difference

Adjective

noun की quality बताता है।

Example:

smart boy

---

Article

noun general है या specific, यह बताता है।

Example:

a boy

the boy

---

Important Rule

अगर article और adjective दोनों हों, तो article पहले आएगा।

---

Example

a tall boy ✅

❌ tall a boy

---

3. Quantifier

(परिमाण बोधक)

English Definition

A quantifier is a word that indicates the amount or quantity of a noun in an indefinite way.

---

Hindi Definition

जो शब्द किसी noun की मात्रा का बोध कराए लेकिन exact संख्या न बताए, उसे quantifier कहते हैं।

---

Examples

some water

many books

few students

much milk

---

Important Understanding

Quantifier: exact counting नहीं देता, सिर्फ quantity का अंदाज़ा देता है।

---

Quantifier vs Numeral

Quantifier

approximate quantity

Examples:

some

many

few

---

Numeral

exact number/order

Examples:

one

two

first

second

---

4. Numeral

(संख्या बोधक)

English Definition

A numeral is a word that indicates the exact number or order of a noun.

---

Hindi Definition

जो शब्द किसी noun की सही संख्या या क्रम का बोध कराए, उसे numeral कहते हैं।

---

Types of Numeral

Cardinal Numeral

Quantity बताता है।

Examples:

one

two

three

---

Ordinal Numeral

Position बताता है।

Examples:

first

second

third

---

Important Understanding

Quantifier: अंदाज़ा

Numeral: exact counting

---

Old Grammar vs Modern Grammar

Old Grammar

सब adjective family के अंदर थे।

---

Modern Grammar

अब:

determiner

article

quantifier

numeral

को अलग functional categories माना जाता है।

---

Why?

क्योंकि:

इनके grammar rules अलग हैं

sentence position अलग है

usage logic अलग है

---

Easy Family Logic

पुराने समय में: adjective एक बड़ा परिवार था।

अब: उसके कुछ “बच्चों” को modern grammar ने अलग पहचान दे दी।

---

Common Mistakes

❌ the this boy

❌ a my book

---

✅ this smart boy

✅ a tall girl

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern linguistics में: determiners को कई बार adjective से भी अलग माना जाता है।

लेकिन traditional grammar में: इन्हें adjective family से जोड़कर पढ़ाया जाता है।

दोनों systems को समझना जरूरी है।

Part 21 — Verb System

(क्रिया प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

noun

pronoun

adjective

समझा।

अब हम grammar के सबसे महत्वपूर्ण parts में से एक: Verb समझेंगे।

क्योंकि: verb के बिना सामान्यतः sentence complete नहीं होता।

Verb:

action

state

happening

को व्यक्त करता है।

---

What is a Verb?

English Definition

The word that expresses an action or a state of being is called a verb.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो किसी कार्य, अवस्था या घटना को बताए, verb कहलाता है।

---

Examples

run → दौड़ना

eat → खाना

write → लिखना

think → सोचना

---

Important Understanding

Verb केवल physical action नहीं बताता।

यह:

मानसिक क्रिया

अवस्था

अस्तित्व

भी बता सकता है।

---

Types of Verb According to Function

1. Action Verb

2. State Verb

---

1. Action Verb

(कार्यवाचक क्रिया)

English Definition

The verb that expresses an action is called an action verb.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb किसी कार्य या क्रिया का बोध कराए, उसे Action Verb कहते हैं।

---

Physical Actions

run → दौड़ना

eat → खाना

beat → मारना

write → लिखना

---

Mental Actions

think → सोचना

understand → समझना

remember → याद रखना

believe → विश्वास करना

---

Example Sentences

He runs fast.

→ वह तेज दौड़ता है।

I understand the lesson.

→ मैं पाठ समझता हूँ।

---

2. State Verb

(अवस्थावाचक क्रिया)

English Definition

The verb that expresses a state or condition is called a state verb.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb किसी अवस्था या स्थिति का बोध कराए, उसे State Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

am

is

are

was

were

---

Example Sentences

He is a boy.

→ वह लड़का है।

She is happy.

→ वह खुश है।

I am a teacher.

→ मैं शिक्षक हूँ।

---

Important Understanding

इन sentences में: कोई action नहीं हो रहा।

Verb: स्थिति/अवस्था बता रहा है।

---

Main Verb

(मुख्य क्रिया)

English Definition

The main verb is the principal verb that expresses the main action or state in a sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb sentence का मुख्य कार्य या मुख्य अवस्था बताए, उसे Main Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

He plays cricket.

यहाँ: plays = main verb

---

She is singing.

यहाँ: singing = main verb

---

Helping Verb / Auxiliary Verb

(सहायक क्रिया)

English Definition

The verb that helps the main verb to form tense, voice, mood, or question is called a helping verb or auxiliary verb.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb मुख्य क्रिया की सहायता करे, उसे Helping Verb या Auxiliary Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

am

is

are

was

were

do

does

did

have

has

had

will

shall

---

Example Sentences

She is singing.

is → helping verb

singing → main verb

---

I have completed my work.

have → helping verb

completed → main verb

---

Important Understanding

Helping verb:

tense बनाने में

question बनाने में

negative sentence बनाने में

मदद करता है।

---

Verb Forms

(क्रिया के रूप)

English verbs सामान्यतः पाँच forms में पढ़े जाते हैं।

---

V1 — Base Form

go

eat

write

---

V2 — Past Form

went

ate

wrote

---

V3 — Past Participle

gone

eaten

written

---

V4 — ING Form

going

eating

writing

---

V5 — S/ES Form

goes

eats

writes

---

Example Table

V1V2V3V4V5

gowentgonegoinggoes

eatateeateneatingeats

writewrotewrittenwritingwrites

---

Finite Verb

(निश्चित क्रिया)

English Definition

A finite verb is a verb that changes according to tense, number, or person.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb tense, number या person के अनुसार बदलती है, उसे Finite Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

He goes to school.

They go to school.

---

Important Understanding

यहाँ: go/goes

subject के अनुसार बदल रहा है।

इसलिए: finite verb

---

Non-Finite Verb

(अनिश्चित क्रिया)

English Definition

A non-finite verb is a verb that does not change according to tense, number, or person.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb tense, number या person के अनुसार नहीं बदलती, उसे Non-Finite Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

To read is good.

Reading is useful.

He likes to swim.

---

Important Understanding

यहाँ: to read

reading

to swim

subject या tense के अनुसार नहीं बदल रहे।

---

Transitive Verb

(सकर्मक क्रिया)

English Definition

The verb that requires an object to complete its meaning is called a transitive verb.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb अपना अर्थ पूरा करने के लिए object माँगे, उसे Transitive Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

He eats mangoes.

---

Explanation

eats → verb

mangoes → object

---

Important Understanding

अगर object हटाएँ:

He eats…

sentence अधूरा लगता है।

---

Intransitive Verb

(अकर्मक क्रिया)

English Definition

The verb that does not require an object to complete its meaning is called an intransitive verb.

---

Hindi Definition

जो verb अपना अर्थ पूरा करने के लिए object न माँगे, उसे Intransitive Verb कहते हैं।

---

Examples

The baby cried.

Birds fly.

---

Important Understanding

यहाँ: कोई object आवश्यक नहीं है।

---

Subject-Verb Agreement

Verb को: subject के number और person के अनुसार बदलना पड़ता है।

---

Examples

He goes to school. ✅

They go to school. ✅

---

He go to school. ❌

---

Important Understanding

Singular Subject

→ singular verb

---

Plural Subject

→ plural verb

---

Be Verb System

Present

am

is

are

---

Past

was

were

---

Future

shall be

will be

---

Example Sentences

I am ready.

She is happy.

They are students.

---

Important Understanding

Be verbs: अक्सर अवस्था, पहचान या स्थिति बताते हैं।

---

Common Mistakes

❌ He go to school.

✅ He goes to school.

---

❌ They is happy.

✅ They are happy.

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern grammar में:

gerund

participle

infinitive

को verb family का विस्तार माना जाता है।

आगे grammar में इन्हें detail में पढ़ेंगे।

Part 22 — Verb Family Expansion

(क्रिया परिवार विस्तार)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, Part 21 में हमने:

main verb

helping verb

action/state verb

transitive/intransitive

finite/non-finite

समझा।

अब हम verb family के advanced members को समझेंगे।

पुराने grammar system में: इन सबको सामान्य verb के अंदर ही पढ़ाया जाता था।

लेकिन modern grammar में: इनके अलग functions की वजह से इन्हें अलग पहचान दी गई।

---

Verb Family Expansion

1. Gerund

2. Participle

3. Infinitive

---

Important Historical Understanding

पुराने समय में: verb एक बहुत बड़ा परिवार था।

लेकिन modern grammar ने देखा कि: कुछ verbs:

noun की तरह

adjective की तरह

special structure की तरह

काम कर रहे हैं।

इसलिए: उन्हें अलग categories दी गई।

---

1. Gerund

(क्रियार्थक संज्ञा)

English Definition

When the “ing” form of a verb is used like a noun in a sentence, it is called a gerund.

---

Hindi Definition

जब verb के “ing” form का प्रयोग sentence में noun की तरह किया जाए, उसे gerund कहते हैं।

---

Basic Formula

Verb + ing

acting like noun

---

Examples

Swimming is my hobby.

---

Explanation

swimming

→ verb का ing form

लेकिन यहाँ: यह noun की तरह काम कर रहा है।

क्यों?

क्योंकि: यह hobby का नाम बन गया है।

---

More Examples

Reading is useful.

→ पढ़ना उपयोगी है।

Walking is good for health.

→ चलना स्वास्थ्य के लिए अच्छा है।

---

Important Understanding

Gerund: काम भी दिखाता है, और noun की तरह भी काम करता है।

---

Verb vs Gerund

Verb

I am swimming.

यहाँ: swimming = action verb

---

Gerund

Swimming is my hobby.

यहाँ: swimming = noun

---

Final Easy Rule

अगर: verb noun की तरह काम करे, तो gerund।

---

2. Participle

(क्रियात्मक विशेषण)

English Definition

A participle is a form of verb that functions as an adjective to describe a noun or pronoun.

---

Hindi Definition

Participle क्रिया का वह रूप है जिसका प्रयोग adjective की तरह noun या pronoun की विशेषता बताने के लिए किया जाता है।

---

Important Understanding

Participle: verb से बना होता है, लेकिन काम adjective का करता है।

---

Examples

The tired man slept.

---

Explanation

tired

→ verb form से बना

लेकिन यहाँ: man की विशेषता बता रहा है।

इसलिए: participle

---

More Examples

A running train

→ दौड़ती हुई ट्रेन

The broken chair

→ टूटी हुई कुर्सी

The crying baby

→ रोता हुआ बच्चा

---

Important Understanding

Participle: noun की condition/quality/action state बताता है।

---

Participle vs Adjective

Adjective

smart boy

---

Participle

running boy

---

Difference

Adjective: सीधा quality बताता है।

Participle: verb से बनकर quality बताता है।

---

Types of Participle

Present Participle

Verb + ing

Examples:

running

crying

swimming

---

Past Participle

V3 form

Examples:

broken

written

tired

---

3. Infinitive

(क्रिया का मूल रूप)

English Definition

An infinitive is the base form of a verb usually preceded by “to”.

---

Hindi Definition

Verb का मूल रूप जो सामान्यतः “to” के साथ प्रयोग किया जाए, infinitive कहलाता है।

---

Basic Formula

to + verb

---

Examples

to go

to eat

to read

to write

---

Example Sentences

I want to play.

She likes to sing.

---

Explanation

to play

to sing

infinitive हैं।

---

Important Understanding

Infinitive: verb का special form है।

यह:

noun

adjective

adverb

की तरह भी काम कर सकता है।

---

Examples

Noun Function

To read is good.

---

Adjective Function

I need a book to read.

---

Adverb Function

He came to help me.

---

Gerund vs Participle vs Infinitive

FormMain Function

GerundVerb acting as noun

ParticipleVerb acting as adjective

InfinitiveTo + verb special structure

---

Easy Family Logic

पुराने समय में: ये सब verb family के अंदर थे।

Modern grammar ने: इनके अलग-अलग functions देखकर इन्हें अलग नाम दे दिए।

---

Verbal Noun

(क्रियार्थक संज्ञा)

जब verb noun की तरह काम करे।

Example:

Swimming is useful.

---

Verbal Adjective

(क्रियात्मक विशेषण)

जब verb adjective की तरह काम करे।

Example:

a running train

---

Non-Finite Verb Awareness

Gerund, participle और infinitive: तीनों non-finite verb family के सदस्य माने जाते हैं।

क्योंकि: ये tense/person के अनुसार नहीं बदलते।

---

Important Understanding

Finite Verb

He goes to school.

---

Non-Finite Verb

Going to school is useful.

---

Common Mistakes

❌ I enjoy to swim.

✅ I enjoy swimming.

---

❌ He is a run boy.

✅ He is a running boy.

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern linguistics में: gerund और participle के कुछ forms overlap भी कर सकते हैं।

लेकिन beginner level पर: function-based understanding सबसे important है।

---

Final Easy Rule

Verb acting like noun

→ gerund

---

Verb acting like adjective

→ participle

---

To + verb structure

→ infinitive

Part 23 — Adverb System Deep Study

(क्रिया-विशेषण प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, Part 19 में हमने adjective पढ़ा था।

अब हम adverb को detail में समझेंगे।

कई students:

adjective और

adverb

को confuse कर देते हैं।

लेकिन: इन दोनों का काम अलग होता है।

---

What is an Adverb?

English Definition

The word that describes a verb, adjective, or another adverb is called an adverb.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो किसी verb, adjective या दूसरे adverb की विशेषता बताए, उसे adverb कहते हैं।

---

Important Understanding

Adjective

noun/pronoun को modify करता है।

---

Adverb

verb

adjective

दूसरे adverb

को modify करता है।

---

1. Adverb Modifying a Verb

Example

He runs quickly.

---

Explanation

runs

→ verb

quickly

→ runs को modify कर रहा है।

इसलिए: quickly = adverb

---

More Examples

She sings beautifully.

→ वह सुंदर गाती है।

They worked hard.

→ उन्होंने मेहनत से काम किया।

---

Important Understanding

यहाँ adverb: काम कैसे हुआ, यह बता रहा है।

---

2. Adverb Modifying an Adjective

Example

He is very smart.

---

Explanation

smart

→ adjective

very

→ smart को modify कर रहा है।

इसलिए: very = adverb

---

More Examples

She is extremely beautiful.

This question is too difficult.

---

Important Understanding

यहाँ adverb: adjective की intensity बढ़ा रहा है।

---

3. Adverb Modifying Another Adverb

Example

He runs very quickly.

---

Explanation

quickly

→ adverb

very

→ quickly को modify कर रहा है।

इसलिए: very भी adverb है।

---

More Examples

She speaks quite softly.

They worked very carefully.

---

Final Easy Rule

Verb को modify करे

→ adverb

---

Adjective को modify करे

→ adverb

---

दूसरे adverb को modify करे

→ adverb

---

Common Ending of Adverbs

अधिकतर adverbs: “ly” से समाप्त होते हैं।

---

Examples

slowly

quickly

beautifully

carefully

---

Important Understanding

लेकिन: सभी adverbs “ly” वाले नहीं होते।

---

Examples

fast

hard

late

well

---

Types of Adverb

अब हम adverb के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

---

1. Adverb of Manner

(रीतिवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

English Definition

The adverb that tells how an action happens is called an adverb of manner.

---

Hindi Definition

जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कैसे हुआ, उसे Adverb of Manner कहते हैं।

---

Examples

slowly

quickly

carefully

beautifully

---

Example Sentences

The boy writes neatly.

She danced beautifully.

---

Question Trick

How?

---

Example

How does he write?

Answer: neatly

---

2. Adverb of Time

(कालवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

English Definition

The adverb that tells when an action happens is called an adverb of time.

---

Hindi Definition

जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कब हुआ, उसे Adverb of Time कहते हैं।

---

Examples

today

tomorrow

yesterday

now

---

Example Sentences

We will go tomorrow.

He came yesterday.

---

Question Trick

When?

---

Example

When will we go?

Answer: tomorrow

---

3. Adverb of Place

(स्थानवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

English Definition

The adverb that tells where an action happens is called an adverb of place.

---

Hindi Definition

जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कहाँ हुआ, उसे Adverb of Place कहते हैं।

---

Examples

here

there

outside

upstairs

---

Example Sentences

Please sit here.

The cat slept upstairs.

---

Question Trick

Where?

---

Example

Where did the cat sleep?

Answer: upstairs

---

4. Adverb of Frequency

(आवृत्तिवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

English Definition

The adverb that tells how often an action happens is called an adverb of frequency.

---

Hindi Definition

जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कितनी बार होता है, उसे Adverb of Frequency कहते हैं।

---

Examples

always

often

sometimes

never

---

Example Sentences

He always speaks the truth.

She never drinks tea.

---

Question Trick

How often?

---

5. Adverb of Degree

(परिमाणवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

English Definition

The adverb that tells the intensity or degree of something is called an adverb of degree.

---

Hindi Definition

जो adverb किसी कार्य, गुण या अवस्था की मात्रा या तीव्रता बताए, उसे Adverb of Degree कहते हैं।

---

Examples

very

too

quite

extremely

---

Example Sentences

She is very smart.

This box is too heavy.

---

Adverb Position

Adverb sentence में अलग-अलग स्थान पर आ सकता है।

---

Beginning

Yesterday, I met him.

---

Middle

He always comes late.

---

End

She sings beautifully.

---

Important Understanding

Adverb की position: उसके type और emphasis पर depend करती है।

---

Adjective vs Adverb

AdjectiveAdverb

noun/pronoun modify करता हैverb/adjective/adverb modify करता है

smart boyruns quickly

---

Examples

He is a quick runner.

→ quick = adjective

He runs quickly.

→ quickly = adverb

---

Important Understanding

Adjective

कैसा?

---

Adverb

कैसे? कब? कहाँ? कितनी बार?

---

Multiple Adverbs in One Sentence

Example

The tired cat slept quietly upstairs.

---

Explanation

quietly

→ कैसे सोया?

upstairs

→ कहाँ सोया?

---

Important Understanding

एक sentence में: एक से अधिक adverbs हो सकते हैं।

---

Common Mistakes

❌ He runs quick.

✅ He runs quickly.

---

❌ She sings beautiful.

✅ She sings beautifully.

---

Exception Awareness

कुछ words: adjective और adverb दोनों हो सकते हैं।

---

Examples

fast

hard

late

---

Example Sentences

He is a fast runner.

→ adjective

He runs fast.

→ adverb

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern grammar में: कुछ grammarians adverbs को:

sentence adverb

focusing adverb

linking adverb

जैसी categories में भी बाँटते हैं।

आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

Part 24 — Preposition System

(संबंध बोधक अव्यय प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

noun

pronoun

adjective

verb

adverb

समझा।

अब हम preposition समझेंगे।

Sentence में केवल words होना काफी नहीं होता।

उनके बीच:

relation

position

direction

time

भी बताना पड़ता है।

यही काम preposition करता है।

---

What is a Preposition?

English Definition

A word placed before a noun, pronoun, or noun phrase to show its relation with another part of the sentence is called a preposition.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो noun, pronoun या noun phrase से पहले आकर उसका संबंध sentence के दूसरे शब्दों से जोड़ता है, preposition कहलाता है।

---

Important Understanding

Preposition: दो words या groups के बीच relation दिखाता है।

---

Examples

in

on

at

to

with

under

over

beside

between

---

Example Sentences

The book is on the table.

Ram is in the room.

She sat beside me.

---

Relation Logic

Preposition सामान्यतः बताता है:

कहाँ?

कब?

किस दिशा में?

किसके साथ?

किसके ऊपर/नीचे?

---

Types of Preposition

अब हम preposition के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

---

1. Preposition of Place

(स्थान बोधक संबंध)

English Definition

The preposition that shows place or position is called a preposition of place.

---

Hindi Definition

जो preposition किसी स्थान या स्थिति का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Place कहते हैं।

---

Examples

in

on

under

behind

beside

---

Example Sentences

The cat is under the table.

The picture is on the wall.

Ram is in the classroom.

---

Important Understanding

in

अंदर

---

on

ऊपर (touching surface)

---

under

नीचे

---

2. Preposition of Time

(समय बोधक संबंध)

English Definition

The preposition that shows time is called a preposition of time.

---

Hindi Definition

जो preposition समय का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Time कहते हैं।

---

Main Time Prepositions

at

on

in

---

Use of “At”

Specific time

---

Examples

at 5 o’clock

at night

---

Use of “On”

Specific day/date

---

Examples

on Monday

on 15 August

---

Use of “In”

Longer periods

---

Examples

in 2025

in winter

in the morning

---

Final Easy Rule

At

exact time

---

On

day/date

---

In

month/year/long period

---

3. Preposition of Direction

(दिशा बोधक संबंध)

English Definition

The preposition that shows movement or direction is called a preposition of direction.

---

Hindi Definition

जो preposition दिशा या movement का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Direction कहते हैं।

---

Examples

to

towards

into

onto

---

Example Sentences

He went to school.

The boy jumped into the river.

She walked towards the market.

---

Important Understanding

Direction prepositions: movement दिखाते हैं।

---

4. Preposition of Cause or Purpose

(कारण/उद्देश्य बोधक संबंध)

English Definition

The preposition that shows reason or purpose is called a preposition of cause or purpose.

---

Hindi Definition

जो preposition कारण या उद्देश्य का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Cause/Purpose कहते हैं।

---

Examples

for

because of

due to

---

Example Sentences

He was punished for his mistake.

The match was cancelled because of rain.

---

Preposition + Noun Phrase

Preposition सामान्यतः noun phrase के साथ आता है।

---

Examples

on the table

in the classroom

under the old tree

---

Important Understanding

Preposition के बाद:

noun

pronoun

noun phrase

आता है।

---

Preposition vs Adverb

कई बार same word:

preposition या

adverb

दोनों हो सकता है।

---

Example 1

He went inside the room.

inside + noun

→ preposition

---

Example 2

He went inside.

noun नहीं है

→ adverb

---

Important Understanding

Preposition

के बाद object आता है।

---

Adverb

के बाद object जरूरी नहीं।

---

Important Preposition Difference

In vs Into

In

स्थिति

The boy is in the room.

---

Into

movement अंदर की ओर

The boy went into the room.

---

On vs Onto

On

स्थिति

The book is on the table.

---

Onto

movement ऊपर की ओर

The cat jumped onto the table.

---

Between vs Among

Between

दो के बीच

The ball is between Ram and Mohan.

---

Among

कई लोगों/वस्तुओं के बीच

He was sitting among friends.

---

Common Mistakes

❌ He discussed about the issue.

✅ He discussed the issue.

---

❌ She entered into the room.

✅ She entered the room.

---

Fixed Preposition Awareness

कुछ verbs/adjectives के साथ fixed prepositions आते हैं।

---

Examples

interested in

good at

afraid of

depend on

---

Example Sentences

She is interested in music.

He is good at English.

---

Prepositional Phrase

English Definition

A group of words beginning with a preposition and ending with its object is called a prepositional phrase.

---

Hindi Definition

शब्दों का वह समूह जो preposition से शुरू होकर उसके object पर समाप्त हो, prepositional phrase कहलाता है।

---

Examples

in the room

under the table

beside the river

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern grammar में: कुछ grammarians prepositions को:

simple preposition

compound preposition

phrase preposition

में भी बाँटते हैं।

आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

Part 25 — Conjunction System

(समुच्चय बोधक अव्यय प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

noun

pronoun

adjective

verb

adverb

preposition

समझा।

अब हम conjunction समझेंगे।

Sentence में कई बार:

words

phrases

clauses

को जोड़ना पड़ता है।

यही काम conjunction करता है।

---

What is a Conjunction?

English Definition

The word that is used to connect words, phrases, or clauses is called a conjunction.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द जो दो शब्दों, वाक्यांशों या उपवाक्यों को जोड़ने का कार्य करे, conjunction कहलाता है।

---

Important Understanding

Conjunction: एक bond या connection की तरह काम करता है।

---

Connecting Words

tea and coffee

Ram and Shyam

---

Connecting Phrases

on the table or under the table

---

Connecting Clauses

I wanted to go, but it was raining.

---

Types of Conjunction

अब हम conjunction के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

---

1. Coordinating Conjunction

(समन्वयी समुच्चयबोधक)

English Definition

The conjunction that joins words, phrases, or clauses of equal importance is called a coordinating conjunction.

---

Hindi Definition

जो conjunction समान महत्व वाले words, phrases या clauses को जोड़े, उसे Coordinating Conjunction कहते हैं।

---

Main Coordinating Conjunctions

and

but

or

so

for

nor

yet

---

Functions of Coordinating Conjunction

Addition

and

---

Examples

Ram and Shyam

Tea and coffee

---

Contrast

but / yet

---

Examples

He is rich but unhappy.

She is wise yet humble.

---

Choice

or

---

Examples

Tea or coffee

You can stay or leave.

---

Result

so

---

Examples

It was raining, so we stayed home.

---

Important Understanding

Coordinating conjunction: दो equal level के parts को जोड़ता है।

---

2. Subordinating Conjunction

(आश्रित समुच्चयबोधक)

English Definition

The conjunction that joins a dependent clause to an independent clause is called a subordinating conjunction.

---

Hindi Definition

जो conjunction dependent clause को independent clause से जोड़े, उसे Subordinating Conjunction कहते हैं।

---

Examples

because

if

when

although

since

while

---

Example Sentences

I stayed home because it was raining.

When the teacher came, the students stood up.

---

Clause Understanding

Independent Clause

जो अकेले पूरा meaning दे सके।

Example:

I stayed home.

---

Dependent Clause

जो अकेले पूरा meaning न दे सके।

Example:

because it was raining

---

Important Understanding

Subordinating conjunction: एक clause को दूसरे पर dependent बनाता है।

---

3. Correlative Conjunction

(सहसंबंधी समुच्चयबोधक)

English Definition

The conjunctions that work in pairs are called correlative conjunctions.

---

Hindi Definition

जो conjunction जोड़े में कार्य करें, उन्हें Correlative Conjunction कहते हैं।

---

Examples

either…or

neither…nor

both…and

not only…but also

---

Example Sentences

Either Ram or Mohan will come.

Neither the teacher nor the students were ready.

Both tea and coffee are available.

---

Important Understanding

Correlative conjunction: pair में काम करता है।

---

Conjunction vs Preposition

Conjunction

clauses/words जोड़ता है।

Example:

I was tired but I worked.

---

Preposition

noun/pronoun से relation दिखाता है।

Example:

He sat on the chair.

---

Conjunction vs Relative Pronoun

Relative Pronoun

noun + clause जोड़ता है।

Example:

The boy who came here is my friend.

---

Conjunction

दो clauses जोड़ता है।

Example:

I came because you called me.

---

Important Understanding

Relative pronoun: noun का relation बनाता है।

Conjunction: clause connection बनाता है।

---

Common Conjunction Functions

FunctionConjunction

Additionand

Contrastbut

Choiceor

Causebecause

Conditionif

Timewhen

Resultso

---

Multiple Conjunction Example

Although he was tired, he continued working because he wanted success.

---

Explanation

although

→ contrast

because

→ cause

---

Important Understanding

एक sentence में: एक से अधिक conjunction हो सकते हैं।

---

Common Mistakes

❌ Because he was ill.

→ incomplete sentence

✅ He stayed home because he was ill.

---

❌ Although he is rich but unhappy.

✅ Although he is rich, he is unhappy.

✅ He is rich but unhappy.

---

Conjunction and Sentence Building

Conjunction: simple sentences को:

longer

smoother

logical

बनाता है।

---

Example

Simple

Ram came. Mohan came.

---

With Conjunction

Ram and Mohan came.

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern grammar में: कुछ conjunctions को:

coordinating markers

subordinators

discourse connectors

जैसे नामों से भी पढ़ाया जाता है।

आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

Part 26 — Interjection System

(विस्मयादिबोधक प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

noun

pronoun

adjective

verb

adverb

preposition

conjunction

समझा।

अब हम interjection समझेंगे।

English में कई बार:

खुशी

दुख

दर्द

आश्चर्य

गुस्सा

डर

जैसी अचानक भावनाएँ व्यक्त करनी पड़ती हैं।

इन्हें व्यक्त करने के लिए: interjection का प्रयोग किया जाता है।

---

What is an Interjection?

English Definition

A word or phrase used to express sudden emotion without adding grammatical meaning to the sentence is called an interjection.

---

Hindi Definition

वह शब्द या शब्द समूह जो अचानक उत्पन्न भावना या आवेग को व्यक्त करे, लेकिन sentence में कोई grammatical meaning न जोड़े, interjection कहलाता है।

---

Important Understanding

Interjection: grammar structure का मुख्य भाग नहीं होता।

यह: speaker की feeling/emotion दिखाता है।

---

Common Emotions Expressed by Interjection

joy

surprise

pain

sorrow

anger

greeting

approval

disgust

---

1. Interjection of Joy

(खुशी)

Examples

Hurray!

Hurrah!

Wow!

---

Example Sentences

Hurray! We won the match.

Wow! This is amazing.

---

Explanation

यहाँ: interjection अचानक खुशी व्यक्त कर रहा है।

---

2. Interjection of Surprise

(आश्चर्य)

Examples

Oh!

Wow!

What!

---

Example Sentences

Wow! What a beautiful house!

Oh! I did not know that.

---

Explanation

यहाँ: speaker की surprise दिखाई जा रही है।

---

3. Interjection of Pain

(दर्द)

Examples

Ouch!

Ah!

Alas!

---

Example Sentences

Ouch! The pin pricked me.

Ah! My leg hurts.

---

Explanation

यहाँ: interjection अचानक दर्द व्यक्त कर रहा है।

---

4. Interjection of Sorrow

(दुःख)

Examples

Alas!

Oh no!

---

Example Sentences

Alas! He is dead.

Oh no! We lost the game.

---

Explanation

यहाँ: दुःख या अफसोस व्यक्त हो रहा है।

---

5. Interjection of Greeting

(अभिवादन)

Examples

Hello!

Hi!

Good morning!

---

Example Sentences

Hello! How are you?

Good morning! Students.

---

6. Interjection of Approval

(प्रशंसा/स्वीकृति)

Examples

Bravo!

Excellent!

---

Example Sentences

Bravo! You did well.

Excellent! Your answer is correct.

---

Important Understanding

Interjection: sentence के बाकी grammar structure से अलग भी खड़ा हो सकता है।

---

Examples

Wow!

Amazing!

Oops!

---

Interjection and Punctuation

Interjection के बाद सामान्यतः: exclamation mark (!)

लगाया जाता है।

---

Examples

Hurray!

Ouch!

Wow!

---

Important Understanding

Exclamation mark: strong emotion दिखाता है।

---

Interjection vs Normal Sentence

Interjection

Wow!

---

Normal Sentence

This house is very beautiful.

---

Difference

Interjection: emotion directly व्यक्त करता है।

Normal sentence: complete information देता है।

---

Interjection in Spoken English

Spoken English में: interjections communication को:

natural

expressive

emotional

बनाते हैं।

---

Examples

Oops! I forgot my book.

Hey! Listen to me.

Well! Let us start.

---

Common Mistakes

❌ Hurray we won the match

✅ Hurray! We won the match.

---

❌ Wow what a beautiful place

✅ Wow! What a beautiful place!

---

Important Understanding

Interjection: sentence में meaning add नहीं करता, लेकिन emotion add करता है।

---

Small Advanced Awareness

Modern grammar में: कुछ grammarians interjections को:

discourse marker

emotional marker

conversational expression

की तरह भी study करते हैं।

आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

Part 27 — Number, Person, Agreement & Sentence Drill System

(वचन, पुरुष, सामंजस्य एवं वाक्य अभ्यास प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

noun

pronoun

adjective

verb

adverb

preposition

conjunction

interjection

समझ लिया।

अब हम grammar के उस भाग में प्रवेश कर रहे हैं जहाँ:

sentence बनाना

translation करना

spoken English शुरू करना

वास्तविक रूप से शुरू होगा।

यह भाग: grammar और spoken English के बीच का bridge है।

---

Number System

(वचन प्रणाली)

English Definition

The counting of things is called number.

---

Hindi Definition

वस्तुओं की गिनती को number या वचन कहते हैं।

---

Types of Number

1. Singular Number

2. Plural Number

---

Singular Number

(एकवचन)

English Definition

The noun that refers to one person, place, thing, idea, or quality is called singular number.

---

Hindi Definition

जो noun एक व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का बोध कराए, उसे singular number कहते हैं।

---

Examples

boy

girl

book

apple

---

Plural Number

(बहुवचन)

English Definition

The noun that refers to more than one person, place, thing, idea, or quality is called plural number.

---

Hindi Definition

जो noun एक से अधिक व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का बोध कराए, उसे plural number कहते हैं।

---

Examples

boys

girls

books

apples

---

Person System

(पुरुष प्रणाली)

Sentence में:

बोलने वाला

सुनने वाला

जिसके बारे में बात हो रही है

इनके आधार पर person तय होता है।

---

Types of Person

1. First Person

2. Second Person

3. Third Person

---

First Person

(उत्तम पुरुष)

जो बोलता है।

Examples:

I

We

---

Second Person

(मध्यम पुरुष)

जिससे बात की जाए।

Example:

You

---

Third Person

(अन्य पुरुष)

जिसके बारे में बात की जाए।

Examples:

He

She

It

They

Ram

---

Subject-Verb Agreement

(कर्ता-क्रिया सामंजस्य)

English Definition

The verb must agree with its subject in number and person.

---

Hindi Definition

Verb को अपने subject के number और person के अनुसार बदलना पड़ता है।

---

Present Form Agreement

SubjectVerb

I/We/You/Theygo

He/She/Itgoes

---

Examples

I go to school.

He goes to school.

We play cricket.

She plays cricket.

---

Past Form Agreement

Past form सामान्यतः सभी subjects के साथ same रहती है।

---

Examples

I went to school.

He went to school.

They went to school.

---

Be Verb System

Present Form

SubjectBe Verb

Iam

He/She/Itis

We/You/Theyare

---

Examples

I am happy.

He is ready.

They are students.

---

Past Form

SubjectBe Verb

I/He/She/Itwas

We/You/Theywere

---

Examples

She was absent.

They were tired.

---

Future Form

SubjectBe Verb

I/Weshall be / will be

He/She/It/You/Theywill be

---

Examples

I shall be ready.

He will be happy.

They will be successful.

---

Helping Verb System

Present

do

does

have

has

---

Past

did

had

---

Examples

I do my work.

He does his homework.

She has a car.

They had a meeting.

---

Sentence Forms

(वाक्य के प्रकार)

---

1. Affirmative Sentence

(सकारात्मक वाक्य)

English Definition

A sentence that makes a positive statement is called an affirmative sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

जो वाक्य सामान्य सकारात्मक कथन दे, उसे affirmative sentence कहते हैं।

---

Examples

I am happy.

He plays cricket.

They are students.

---

2. Negative Sentence

(नकारात्मक वाक्य)

English Definition

A sentence that expresses negation is called a negative sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

जो वाक्य निषेध या इंकार व्यक्त करे, उसे negative sentence कहते हैं।

---

Examples

I am not happy.

He does not play cricket.

They are not students.

---

3. Interrogative Sentence

(प्रश्नवाचक वाक्य)

English Definition

A sentence that asks a question is called an interrogative sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

जो वाक्य प्रश्न पूछे, उसे interrogative sentence कहते हैं।

---

Examples

Am I happy?

Does he play cricket?

Are they students?

---

4. Interrogative Negative Sentence

(नकारात्मक प्रश्नवाचक वाक्य)

English Definition

A sentence that is both interrogative and negative is called an interrogative negative sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

जो वाक्य प्रश्न और निषेध दोनों व्यक्त करे, उसे interrogative negative sentence कहते हैं।

---

Examples

Am I not happy?

Does he not play cricket?

Are they not students?

---

Short Answer System

Examples

Are you ready?

→ Yes, I am.

→ No, I am not.

---

Is he happy?

→ Yes, he is.

→ No, he is not.

---

Contracted Forms

(Short Spoken Forms)

Examples

I am → I’m

He is → He’s

They are → They’re

do not → don’t

does not → doesn’t

is not → isn’t

are not → aren’t

---

Important Understanding

Contracted forms: spoken English को natural बनाते हैं।

---

Basic Translation Drill System

अब हम एक ही pattern से: सैकड़ों sentences बनाना सीखेंगे।

---

Pattern 1 — “Good”

Affirmative

I am good.

मैं अच्छा हूँ।

We are good.

हम अच्छे हैं।

You are good.

तुम अच्छे हो।

He is good.

वह अच्छा है।

She is good.

वह अच्छी है।

It is good.

यह अच्छा है।

They are good.

वे अच्छे हैं।

---

Negative

I am not good.

मैं अच्छा नहीं हूँ।

We are not good.

हम अच्छे नहीं हैं।

He is not good.

वह अच्छा नहीं है।

She is not good.

वह अच्छी नहीं है।

They are not good.

वे अच्छे नहीं हैं।

---

Interrogative

Am I good?

क्या मैं अच्छा हूँ?

Are we good?

क्या हम अच्छे हैं?

Are you good?

क्या तुम अच्छे हो?

Is he good?

क्या वह अच्छा है?

Is she good?

क्या वह अच्छी है?

Are they good?

क्या वे अच्छे हैं?

---

Interrogative Negative

Am I not good?

क्या मैं अच्छा नहीं हूँ?

Is he not good?

क्या वह अच्छा नहीं है?

Are they not good?

क्या वे अच्छे नहीं हैं?

---

WH Question System

What

→ क्या

What are you doing?

---

Who

→ कौन

Who are you?

---

When

→ कब

When will you come?

---

Where

→ कहाँ

Where do you live?

---

Why

→ क्यों

Why are you sad?

---

How

→ कैसे

How are you?

---

Which

→ कौन-सा

Which book is yours?

---

Whose

→ किसका

Whose pen is this?

---

Whom

→ किसे / किसको

Whom did you call?

---

WH Pattern Drill

How am I good?

मैं कैसे अच्छा हूँ?

How are we good?

हम कैसे अच्छे हैं?

How are you good?

तुम कैसे अच्छे हो?

How is he good?

वह कैसे अच्छा है?

How is she good?

वह कैसे अच्छी है?

How are they good?

वे कैसे अच्छे हैं?

---

WH Negative Drill

Why am I not ready?

मैं तैयार क्यों नहीं हूँ?

How is she not happy?

वह खुश क्यों नहीं है?

Why are they not present?

वे उपस्थित क्यों नहीं हैं?

---

Substitution Drill System

अब एक ही pattern में word बदलकर सैकड़ों sentence बनाए जाएँगे।

---

Example Words

good

bad

happy

sad

ready

busy

hungry

tired

---

Examples

I am happy.

He is busy.

They are tired.

---

Daily Use Sentence Bank

Emotion

I am happy.

She is sad.

---

Need

I need water.

He needs help.

---

Ability

I can swim.

She can dance.

---

Basic Command & Request

Come here.

Sit down.

Please help me.

---

Basic Modal Verb Awareness

can

may

should

must

---

Examples

I can swim.

You should study.

We must work hard.

---

Word Order Rule

English में सामान्य word order:

Subject + Verb + Object

---

Examples

I play cricket.

She reads books.

---

Wrong vs Right

❌ I good am.

✅ I am good.

---

❌ He go to school.

✅ He goes to school.

---

❌ Does he goes?

✅ Does he go?

---

Mini Conversation Drill

How are you?

→ I am fine.

Where do you live?

→ I live in Patna.

What do you do?

→ I am a teacher.

---

Vocabulary Integration Strategy

अब vocabulary को अलग से नहीं, patterns के अंदर सिखाया जाएगा।

---

Example Vocabulary Group

Emotion Words

happy

sad

angry

tired

---

Pattern

I am happy.

She is tired.

They are angry.

---

Important Understanding

जब vocabulary: grammar patterns में repeatedly use होती है, तो:

जल्दी याद होती है

speaking में automatically आने लगती है

translation आसान हो जाता है।

---

Final Goal of Part 27

Student:

sentence बनाना शुरू करे

grammar को apply करे

translation करे

spoken English शुरू करे

patterns को पहचानकर नए sentences बना सके।

Part 28 — Sentence Construction & Spoken Drill System

(वाक्य निर्माण एवं बोलचाल अभ्यास प्रणाली)

Teacher Introduction

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

parts of speech

verb system

agreement system

helping verb

WH words

sentence forms

समझ लिया।

अब हम grammar को वास्तविक English में बदलेंगे।

यही वह भाग है जहाँ: student को पहली बार लगेगा:

“Yes, I can speak English.”

What is a Sentence?

English Definition

A group of words that expresses a complete thought is called a sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

शब्दों का ऐसा समूह जो पूरा अर्थ दे, sentence कहलाता है।

---

Examples

I am ready.

मैं तैयार हूँ।

She is happy.

वह खुश है।

They play cricket.

वे क्रिकेट खेलते हैं।

---

Important Understanding

Sentence में सामान्यतः:

subject

verb

जरूरी होते हैं।

---

Basic Sentence Formula

Subject + Verb + Object

---

Examples

I play cricket.

She reads books.

They eat mangoes.

---

Spoken Drill System

अब हम: एक ही structure को:

person

number

tense

question

negative

में घुमाकर practice करेंगे।

इसे: Pattern Rotation Drill कहेंगे।

---

Pattern 1 — “Go”

Present Affirmative

I go.

मैं जाता हूँ।

We go.

हम जाते हैं।

You go.

तुम जाते हो।

He goes.

वह जाता है।

She goes.

वह जाती है।

It goes.

यह जाता है।

They go.

वे जाते हैं।

---

Present Negative

I do not go.

मैं नहीं जाता हूँ।

We do not go.

हम नहीं जाते हैं।

He does not go.

वह नहीं जाता है।

She does not go.

वह नहीं जाती है।

They do not go.

वे नहीं जाते हैं।

---

Present Interrogative

Do I go?

क्या मैं जाता हूँ?

Do we go?

क्या हम जाते हैं?

Do you go?

क्या तुम जाते हो?

Does he go?

क्या वह जाता है?

Does she go?

क्या वह जाती है?

Do they go?

क्या वे जाते हैं?

---

Present Interrogative Negative

Do I not go?

क्या मैं नहीं जाता हूँ?

Does he not go?

क्या वह नहीं जाता है?

Do they not go?

क्या वे नहीं जाते हैं?

---

WH Question Drill

Why do I go?

मैं क्यों जाता हूँ?

Where does he go?

वह कहाँ जाता है?

When do they go?

वे कब जाते हैं?

How does she go?

वह कैसे जाती है?

---

WH Negative Drill

Why do I not go?

मैं क्यों नहीं जाता हूँ?

Why does he not go?

वह क्यों नहीं जाता है?

---

Pattern 2 — “Good”

Present Affirmative

I am good.

मैं अच्छा हूँ।

We are good.

हम अच्छे हैं।

You are good.

तुम अच्छे हो।

He is good.

वह अच्छा है।

She is good.

वह अच्छी है।

It is good.

यह अच्छा है।

They are good.

वे अच्छे हैं।

---

Negative

I am not good.

He is not good.

They are not good.

---

Interrogative

Am I good?

Is he good?

Are they good?

---

Interrogative Negative

Am I not good?

Is she not good?

Are they not good?

---

WH Drill

How am I good?

Why is he good?

Where are they good?

---

Past Pattern Drill

“Go”

I went.

मैं गया।

He went.

वह गया।

They went.

वे गए।

---

Negative

I did not go.

He did not go.

They did not go.

---

Interrogative

Did I go?

Did he go?

Did they go?

---

Past Be Verb Pattern

I was ready.

He was happy.

They were busy.

---

Future Pattern Drill

I shall go.

He will go.

They will go.

---

Negative

I shall not go.

He will not go.

---

Interrogative

Shall I go?

Will he go?

Will they go?

---

Future Be Verb Pattern

I shall be ready.

He will be successful.

They will be happy.

---

Massive Substitution Drill

अब: एक ही structure में: word बदलकर सैकड़ों sentence बनाए जाएँगे।

---

Examples

I play.

He plays.

---

Negative

I do not play.

He does not play.

---

Question

Do you play?

Does he play?

Daily Life Sentence Drill

Emotion

I am sad.

She is angry.

---

Need

I need water.

He needs money.

---

Ability

I can swim.

She can dance.

---

Possession

I have a pen.

They have books.

---

Spoken English Mini Conversation

Greeting

How are you?

→ I am fine.

---

Identity

What is your name?

→ My name is Ram.

---

Place

Where do you live?

→ I live in Patna.

---

Work

What do you do?

→ I am a teacher.

---

Command Sentence

(आज्ञासूचक वाक्य)

English Definition

A sentence that expresses command, order, advice, or request is called an imperative sentence.

---

Hindi Definition

जो वाक्य आदेश, अनुरोध, सलाह या निर्देश दे, उसे imperative sentence कहते हैं।

---

Examples

Sit down.

Come here.

Please help me.

Study hard.

---

Modal Verb Spoken Drill

can

may

should

must

---

Examples

I can swim.

You should study.

We must work hard.

May I come in?

---

Short Answer System

Are you ready?

→ Yes, I am.

→ No, I am not.

---

Do you play cricket?

→ Yes, I do.

→ No, I do not.

---

Contracted Forms

I am → I’m

He is → He’s

They are → They’re

do not → don’t

does not → doesn’t

will not → won’t

---

Error Detection System

❌ He go to school.

✅ He goes to school.

---

❌ Does he goes?

✅ Does he go?

---

❌ I good am.

✅ I am good.

---

---

Example

happy

sad

hungry

busy

---

Pattern Practice

I am happy.

She is busy.

They are hungry.

---

Important Understanding

जब vocabulary: grammar pattern के अंदर repeatedly use होती है, तो:

जल्दी याद होती है

बोलने में आने लगती है

translation आसान हो जाता है।

Latest Strategic Suggestions

1. Add “Memory Revision Blocks”

After every 3–4 parts: add:

recap drill

mixed translation

rapid-fire correction

This prevents overload.

---

2. Add “Mistake Psychology”

Example:

❌ He go

✅ He goes

Explain: WHY brain creates this mistake.

This is extremely powerful.

---

3. Add “Hindi Thinking Trap”

Example:

मैं अच्छा हूँ

NOT: ❌ I good am

Explain: Hindi order vs English order.

Very important for Hindi-medium learners.

---

4. Add “Speaking Speed Layers”

Level 1: slow pattern

Level 2: normal

Level 3: fast spoken repetition

This will dramatically improve fluency.

---

5. Add “Real Life Vocabulary Clusters”

Instead of random words.

Example:

School Cluster

teacher student classroom homework exam

Then sentence drill.

This is much stronger psychologically.

---

6. Add “Micro Conversation Engine”

Tiny real conversations after each chapter.

Example:

Where do you live?

I live in Patna.

What do you do?

I am a teacher.

This creates practical confidence early.

---

7. Most Important Future Upgrade

Tense Frequency Priority System

Do NOT teach all tenses equally.

Teach:

real spoken tenses first

low-frequency tenses later

This is a major modern teaching advantage.

Part 29 — Tense System

बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

sentence structure

समझ लिया।

अब हम English grammar के सबसे महत्वपूर्ण systems में से एक: Tense System समझेंगे।

क्योंकि: tense हमें बताता है:

काम कब हुआ

कब हो रहा है

कब होगा

---

What is Tense?

English Definition

A tense is a form of verb that shows the time of an action or state.

---

Hindi Definition

Verb का वह रूप जो किसी कार्य या अवस्था का समय बताए, tense कहलाता है।

---

Types of Tense

1. Present Tense

2. Past Tense

3. Future Tense

---

Timeline Logic

Present

अभी

---

Past

बीता हुआ समय

---

Future

आने वाला समय

---

Tense Structure System

प्रत्येक tense के सामान्यतः चार भाग होते हैं:

1. Simple

2. Continuous

3. Perfect

4. Perfect Continuous

---

Full Tense Chart

TimeSimpleContinuousPerfectPerfect Continuous

PresentPresent IndefinitePresent ContinuousPresent PerfectPresent Perfect Continuous

PastPast IndefinitePast ContinuousPast PerfectPast Perfect Continuous

FutureFuture IndefiniteFuture ContinuousFuture PerfectFuture Perfect Continuous

---

Most Important Strategy

सभी tenses को एक साथ बराबर importance नहीं दिया जाएगा।

पहले: daily spoken tenses

फिर: advanced/rare tenses।

---

Most Frequently Used Tenses

Highest Priority

1. Present Indefinite

2. Present Continuous

3. Past Indefinite

4. Future Indefinite

5. Present Perfect

---

Least Priority Initially

Future Perfect Continuous

Past Perfect Continuous

क्योंकि: daily life में कम उपयोग होते हैं।

---

1. Present Indefinite Tense

(Simple Present)

Main Use

daily habit

routine

universal truth

repeated action

---

Structure

Affirmative

Subject + V1/V5 + Object

---

Examples

I play cricket.

मैं क्रिकेट खेलता हूँ।

He goes to school.

वह स्कूल जाता है।

The sun rises in the east.

सूर्य पूर्व में उगता है।

---

Negative Structure

Subject + do/does + not + V1

---

Examples

I do not play cricket.

He does not go to school.

---

Interrogative Structure

Do/Does + Subject + V1?

---

Examples

Do you play cricket?

Does he go to school?

---

WH Structure

WH + do/does + subject + V1?

---

Examples

Why do you study?

Where does he live?

---

Important Agreement Rule

He/She/It

→ V5

---

Examples

He plays.

She writes.

---

But

I play.

They play.

---

2. Present Continuous Tense

Main Use

जो काम अभी इस समय चल रहा हो।

---

Structure

Subject + am/is/are + V4

---

Examples

I am reading.

She is singing.

They are playing.

---

Negative

Subject + am/is/are + not + V4

---

Examples

I am not reading.

He is not sleeping.

---

Interrogative

Am/Is/Are + Subject + V4?

---

Examples

Are you reading?

Is she dancing?

---

WH Pattern

What are you doing?

Why is he crying?

---

Important Understanding

Continuous tense: चल रहे action को दिखाता है।

---

3. Past Indefinite Tense

Main Use

बीते समय में पूरा हुआ कार्य।

---

Structure

Subject + V2

---

Examples

I went home.

She wrote a letter.

They played football.

---

Negative

Subject + did not + V1

---

Examples

I did not go.

He did not play.

---

Interrogative

Did + Subject + V1?

---

Examples

Did you come?

Did she sing?

---

Important Rule

Did के बाद: हमेशा V1 आएगा।

---

Wrong vs Right

❌ Did he went?

✅ Did he go?

---

4. Future Indefinite Tense

Main Use

भविष्य का कार्य।

---

Structure

Subject + shall/will + V1

---

Examples

I shall go.

He will play.

They will come.

---

Negative

Subject + shall/will + not + V1

---

Examples

I shall not go.

She will not sing.

---

Interrogative

Shall/Will + Subject + V1?

---

Examples

Will you come?

Shall I help you?

---

5. Present Perfect Tense

Main Use

जो कार्य अभी-अभी पूरा हुआ हो या जिसका प्रभाव वर्तमान में हो।

---

Structure

Subject + has/have + V3

---

Examples

I have finished my work.

She has written a letter.

They have gone home.

---

Negative

Subject + has/have + not + V3

---

Examples

He has not eaten food.

They have not arrived.

---

Interrogative

Has/Have + Subject + V3?

---

Examples

Have you completed the work?

Has she gone home?

---

Tense Recognition Logic

Daily Habit

→ Present Indefinite

---

Action Going On

→ Present Continuous

---

Completed Past Action

→ Past Indefinite

---

Future Action

→ Future Indefinite

---

Recently Completed

→ Present Perfect

---

Spoken Drill Rotation

Play

I play.

I am playing.

I played.

I will play.

I have played.

---

Negative Rotation

I do not play.

I am not playing.

I did not play.

I will not play.

I have not played.

---

Interrogative Rotation

Do I play?

Am I playing?

Did I play?

Will I play?

Have I played?

---

WH Rotation

Why do I play?

Why am I playing?

Why did I play?

Why will I play?

Why have I played?

---

Time Signal Words

Present Indefinite

daily

always

everyday

---

Present Continuous

now

right now

at present

---

Past

yesterday

last night

ago

---

Future

tomorrow

next week

later

---

Present Perfect

just

already

yet

---

Common Mistakes

❌ He go to school.

✅ He goes to school.

---

❌ I am go.

✅ I am going.

---

❌ Did he went?

✅ Did he go?

---

❌ She have completed the work.

✅ She has completed the work.

---

Most Important Spoken Strategy

Tense को: formula की तरह नहीं, pattern rotation की तरह सीखना है।

---

Example

eat

I eat.

I am eating.

I ate.

I will eat.

I have eaten.

Vocabulary Integration

अब verbs को tense rotation में सिखाया जाएगा।

---

Example Verbs

go

come

eat

play

write

read

speak

Student:

tense पहचान सके

tense बना सके

translation कर सके

spoken English में tense use कर सके

एक verb से multiple tense sentence बना सके।

Teacher Introduction

यह वही layer है: जिससे daily spoken English का सबसे बड़ा भाग बनता है।

अगर यह layer strong हो गई, तो:

translation

speaking

sentence making

tense recognition

बहुत आसान हो जाएगा।

---

What is Tense?

English Definition

A tense is a form of verb that shows the time of an action or state.

---

Hindi Definition

Verb का वह रूप जो किसी कार्य या अवस्था का समय बताए, tense कहलाता है।

---

Main Time Division

TimeMeaning

Presentअभी

Pastबीता हुआ समय

Futureआने वाला समय

---

Most Important Spoken Tenses

इस layer में हम वही tenses पढ़ेंगे: जो daily life में सबसे ज्यादा उपयोग होते हैं।

---

Included Tenses in 29L1

2. Present Continuous

3. Past Indefinite

4. Future Indefinite
